Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Comanche 67, the Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) Command Module (CM) software for Apollo 12.

They have been adapted from sources files for Comanche 55, and updated via disassembly of binary dumps of original core rope memory modules, part numbers 2003972-1081, 2003972-1091, 2003972-1111, 2003972-1121, 2003972-1131, and 2003972-1141.

Since only binary dumps (rather than listings) of Comanche 67 are available as source material, all comments and labels are approximate. They have been taken from other AGC programs where possible, or, in some places, written from scratch to match what we believe would have been in the original listing. 

001487,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
001488,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc
001489,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Comanche revision 067.
001490,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the flight
001491,000006:                                                                                                  ##              software for the Command Module's (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer
001492,000007:                                                                                                  ##              (AGC) for Apollo 12. No original listings of this program are
001493,000008:                                                                                                  ##              available; instead, this file was created via dissassembly of
001494,000009:                                                                                                  ##              dumps of Comanche 067 core rope modules and comparison with
001495,000010:                                                                                                  ##              other AGC programs.
001496,000011:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
001497,000012:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
001498,000013:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
001499,000014:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2023-08-16 MAS  Created from Comanche 055.
001500,000015:                                                                                                  ##              2024-05-13 MAS  Updated for Comanche 067.
001501,000016: 
001502,000017:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001503,000018: 
001504,000019:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001505,000020:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001506,000021:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE.
001507,000022: 
001508,000023:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  START
001509,000024:                                                                                                  #                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001510,000025:                                                                                                  #                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001511,000026: 
001512,000027:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001513,000028:                                                                                                  #                (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001514,000029:                                                                                                  #                 USUALLY NUMERIC, IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D ETC.                )
001515,000030: 
001516,000031:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001517,000032:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE.
001518,000033: 
001519,000034:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  Y
001520,000035: 
001521,000036:                                                                                                  #        =       MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001522,000037:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001523,000038: 
001524,000039:                                                                                                  #                        X       =       Y
001525,000040: 
001526,000041:                                                                                                  #        THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001527,000042:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001528,000043: 
001529,000044:                                                                                                  #                M       REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001530,000045:                                                                                                  #                        B       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001531,000046:                                                                                                  #                                INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001532,000047:                                                                                                  #                        I       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001533,000048:                                                                                                  #                                INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001534,000049:                                                                                                  #                                INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001535,000050: 
001536,000051:                                                                                                  #                SIZE    IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001537,000052: 
001538,000053:                                                                                                  #                N       INDICATES THE NATURE OR PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001539,000054:                                                                                                  #                        PL      MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001540,000055:                                                                                                  #                        DSP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001541,000056:                                                                                                  #                        PRM     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001542,000057:                                                                                                  #                                IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001543,000058:                                                                                                  #                                PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001544,000059:                                                                                                  #                        TMP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001545,000060:                                                                                                  #                                IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001546,000061:                                                                                                  #                                IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001547,000062:                                                                                                  #                                PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001548,000063:                                                                                                  #                                CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS
001549,000064:                                                                                                  #                                IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001550,000065:                                                                                                  #                                IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001551,000066:                                                                                                  #                        IN      MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001552,000067:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001553,000068:                                                                                                  #                        OUT     MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001554,000069:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001555,000070: 
001556,000071: 
001557,000072:                                                                                                  #  SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001558,000073: 
001559,000074: 37,2001                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001560,000075: 37,2001                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001561,000076: 37,2001                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001562,000077: 37,2001                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001563,000078: 37,2001                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001564,000079: 37,2001                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001565,000080: 37,2001                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001566,000081:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001567,000082: 
001568,000083: 37,2001                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001569,000084: 37,2001                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001570,000085: 37,2001                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001571,000086: 37,2001                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001572,000087: 37,2001                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)
001573,000088: 37,2001                        BANKRUPT           EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK.
001574,000089: 37,2001                        BRUPT              EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.
001575,000090: 
001576,000091: 37,2001                        CYR                EQUALS   20                                    
001577,000092: 37,2001                        SR                 EQUALS   21                                    
001578,000093: 37,2001                        CYL                EQUALS   22                                    
001579,000094: 37,2001                        EDOP               EQUALS   23                                    #  EDITS INTERPRETIVE OPERATION CODE PAIRS.
001580,000095: 
001581,000096: 37,2001                        TIME2              EQUALS   24                                    
001582,000097: 37,2001                        TIME1              EQUALS   25                                    
001583,000098: 37,2001                        TIME3              EQUALS   26                                    
001584,000099: 37,2001                        TIME4              EQUALS   27                                    
001585,000100: 37,2001                        TIME5              EQUALS   30                                    
001586,000101: 37,2001                        TIME6              EQUALS   31

001589,000104: 37,2001                        CDUZ               EQUALS   34

001591,000106: 37,2001  0000035               OPTY               =        CDUT

001593,000108: 37,2001  0000036               OPTX               =        CDUS

001606,000121: 
001607,000122: 
001608,000123: 37,2001                        CDUZCMD            EQUALS   52                                    
001609,000124: 37,2001                        CDUTCMD            EQUALS   53                                    #  OPTICS TRUNNION COMMAND (WAS OPTYCMD).
001610,000125: 37,2001  0000053               OPTYCMD            =        CDUTCMD                               
001611,000126: 37,2001  0000053               TVCYAW             EQUALS   CDUTCMD                               #  SPS YAW COMMAND IN TVC MODE.
001612,000127: 37,2001                        CDUSCMD            EQUALS   54                                    #  OPTICS SHAFT COMMAND (WAS OPTXCMD).
001613,000128: 37,2001  0000054               TVCPITCH           EQUALS   CDUSCMD                               #  SPS PITCH COMMAND IN TVC MODE.
001614,000129: 37,2001  0000054               OPTXCMD            =        CDUSCMD                               
001615,000130: 37,2001                        EMSD               EQUALS   55                                    
001616,000131: 37,2001                        THRUST             EQUALS   55                                    
001617,000132: 37,2001                        LEMONM             EQUALS   56                                    
001618,000133: 37,2001                        LOCALARM           EQUALS   57                                    
001619,000134: 37,2001                        BANKALRM           EQUALS   60                                    
001620,000135:

001622,000137: 
001623,000138: 37,2001                        LVSQUARE           EQUALS   34D                                   #  SQUARE OF VECTOR INPUT TO ABVAL AND UNIT
001624,000139: 37,2001                        LV                 EQUALS   36D                                   #  LENGTH OF VECTOR INPUT TO UNIT.
001625,000140: 37,2001                        X1                 EQUALS   38D                                   #  INTERPRETIVE SPECIAL REGISTERS RELATIVE
001626,000141: 37,2001                        X2                 EQUALS   39D                                   #  TO THE WORK AREA.
001627,000142: 37,2001                        S1                 EQUALS   40D

002884,001399:                                                                                                  #  (ITEMP1 THROUGH RUPTREG4)             
002885,001400: 
002886,001401:                                                                                                  #  ANY OF THESE MAY BE USED AS TEMPORARIES DURING INTERRUPT OR WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED. THE ITEMP SERIES
002887,001402:                                                                                                  #  IS USED DURING CALLS TO THE EXECUTIVE AND WAITLIST - THE RUPTREGS ARE NOT.

002936,001451: 
002937,001452:                                                                                                  #  EXEC TEMPORARIES WHICH MAY BE USED BETWEEN CCS NEWJOBS.
002938,001453:                                                                                                  #  (INTB15+ THROUGH RUPTMXM)             (32D)
002939,001454:    0114                        INTB15+            ERASE                                          #  REFLECTS 15TH BIT OF INDEXABLE ADDRESSES

002949,001464:
